" ’’ puche jane par ki kya baithak main kisi tarah kaa prastaav rakhe jane kii maang kii gai, unhone kaha ki bhaajapa kii rajya ikai ‘shashakt or ekikrut’ he
 He said that despite Munde's recent stance, no such proposal was brought to the meeting and it was not even needed

 The budget provided Rs 404 crore for modernization of Arabic Persian madrasas, Rs 486 crore for Arabian schools and Rs 215 crore for grants to 246 arabic-persian madrasas of recognized Alia level
 madrason main rashtriya dhvaj-gaan anivaaryyogi sarkaar ne madrason ko lekar pichley saal agast ke maheene main pehla ahm faisla liya tha

 is film main kerala main lav jehad ke naam par hindu ladakiyon ke dharmantaran kaa mudda uthaaya gaya he

 chaatro ke bich jamkar marpet hui he or kai chaatr-chatraayen jakhmi bhi hue hai

 jeenyu campus ke get par police kii tainaati kii gai he, lekin vishvavidhyalay prashasan ne police ko campus ke bheetar ghusane kii ijaajat nahin di
 Students of left wing and ABVP have gone to Basant Kunj police station and lodged a complaint against the students of each other faction in this case
 aayojakon kaa kahana he ki jeenyu main ho rahe dharmantaran ko rokane ke makasad se campus ke bheetar yah film dikhaai ja rahi thi

 binar postaron ke jariye bijepi or RSS ke khilaaf narebaaji kii gai

 vahaan marpet kii ja rahi he or yah bahut gambhir vishay he

 videsh mantri sushamaa swaraj bhi uski rihaai ke liye prayaas kar rahi hai

 ye din aazaadee kaa parv manaane kaa he, lekin dilli par aatanki hamale kaa suraksha agenciyon ne nayaa alert jari kiya he

 unke nishane par kai pramukh hastiyaan bhi hai

 us samay dilli par kuch napak iraadon kii nazren gadi rahengi

 is babat suraksha agenciyon ne dilli police kaa aagaah bhi kar diya he
